@keyframes heart-pop {
  0% {
    transform: scale(0.5) rotate(-5deg);
    opacity: 0;
  }
  15% {
    transform: scale(1.2) rotate(5deg);
    opacity: 0.9;
  }
  30% {
    transform: scale(0.9) rotate(-3deg);
    opacity: 0.8;
  }
  45% {
    transform: scale(1.1) rotate(3deg);
    opacity: 0.8;
  }
  80% {
    transform: scale(1) rotate(0deg);
    opacity: 0.8;
  }
